<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Historical_personalities">Historical personalities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Technische_Universit%C3%A4t_Darmstadt&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Historical personalities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Chaim_Weizmann" title="Chaim Weizmann">Chaim Weizmann</a>, first President of <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karl_Plagge" title="Karl Plagge">Karl Plagge</a>, recognized as one of the <a href="/wiki/Righteous_Among_the_Nations" title="Righteous Among the Nations">Righteous Among the Nations</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jovanka_Bon%C4%8Di%C4%87-Katerini%C4%87" title="Jovanka Bončić-Katerinić">Jovanka Bončić-Katerinić</a>, first woman to obtain an engineering degree in Germany</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/G%C3%BCnter_Behnisch" title="Günter Behnisch">Günter Behnisch</a>, architect of the <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_(Munich)" title="Olympiastadion (Munich)">Olympiastadion (Munich)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Edmund_Collein" title="Edmund Collein">Edmund Collein</a>, east german architect and town planner</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_R%C3%B6sch" title="Wolfgang Rösch">Wolfgang Rösch</a>, vicar general of the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Limburg" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Limburg">Diocese of Limburg</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Franz-Josef_Kemper" title="Franz-Josef Kemper">Franz-Josef Kemper</a>, Olympic medalist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gerhard_Hennige" title="Gerhard Hennige">Gerhard Hennige</a>, Olympic medalist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Josef_Ganz" title="Josef Ganz">Josef Ganz</a>, jewish automotive engineer and father of the original "<a href="/wiki/Volkswagen" title="Volkswagen">Volkswagen</a>"</li></ul>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:188px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Georg_Cantor_(Portr%C3%A4t).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Georg_Cantor_%28Portr%C3%A4t%29.jpg/186px-Georg_Cantor_%28Portr%C3%A4t%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="186" height="251" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Georg_Cantor_%28Portr%C3%A4t%29.jpg/279px-Georg_Cantor_%28Portr%C3%A4t%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Georg_Cantor_%28Portr%C3%A4t%29.jpg/371px-Georg_Cantor_%28Portr%C3%A4t%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1184" data-file-height="1600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Georg_Cantor_(Portr%C3%A4t).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Georg Cantor</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Science">Science</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Technische_Universit%C3%A4t_Darmstadt&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Science">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Harald_Rose" title="Harald Rose">Harald Rose</a>, physicist and laureate of the <a href="/wiki/Wolf_Prize_in_Physics" title="Wolf Prize in Physics">Wolf Prize in Physics</a> (2011)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Maximilian_Haider" title="Maximilian Haider">Maximilian Haider</a>, physicist and laureate of the <a href="/wiki/Wolf_Prize_in_Physics" title="Wolf Prize in Physics">Wolf Prize in Physics</a> (2011)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Gr%C3%BCnberg" title="Peter Grünberg">Peter Grünberg</a>, physicist and laureate of the <a href="/wiki/Wolf_Prize_in_Physics" title="Wolf Prize in Physics">Wolf Prize in Physics</a> (2007)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Georg_Cantor" title="Georg Cantor">Georg Cantor</a>, created the <a href="/wiki/Set_theory" title="Set theory">set theory</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ernst_Schr%C3%B6der" title="Ernst Schröder">Ernst Schröder</a>, mathematician and known for his monumental lectures on the algebra of logic</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lothar_Collatz" title="Lothar Collatz">Lothar Collatz,</a> mathematician and known for the still unsolved <a href="/wiki/3x_%2B_1_problem" class="mw-redirect" title="3x + 1 problem">3<i>x</i> + 1 problem</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/William_Prager" title="William Prager">William Prager</a>, mathematician and known for <a href="/wiki/Drucker%E2%80%93Prager_yield_criterion" title="Drucker–Prager yield criterion">Drucker–Prager yield criterion</a><sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karl_Hessenberg" title="Karl Hessenberg">Karl Hessenberg</a>, known for the <a href="/wiki/Hessenberg_matrix" title="Hessenberg matrix">Hessenberg matrix</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carl_Adam_Petri" title="Carl Adam Petri">Carl Adam Petri</a>, mathematician and inventor of the <a href="/wiki/Petri_nets" class="mw-redirect" title="Petri nets">Petri nets</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sigurd_Hofmann" title="Sigurd Hofmann">Sigurd Hofmann</a>, physicist and discoverer of the chemical elements <a href="/wiki/Darmstadtium" title="Darmstadtium">darmstadtium</a> (<a href="/wiki/Darmstadtium" title="Darmstadtium">Ds</a>, <a href="/wiki/Atomic_number" title="Atomic number">atomic number</a> 110), <a href="/wiki/Roentgenium" title="Roentgenium">roentgenium</a> (<a href="/wiki/Roentgenium" title="Roentgenium">Rg</a>, 111) and <a href="/wiki/Copernicium" title="Copernicium">copernicium</a> (<a href="/wiki/Copernicium" title="Copernicium">Cn</a>, 112)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Armbruster" title="Peter Armbruster">Peter Armbruster</a>, physicist and discoverer of the elements 107 (<a href="/wiki/Bohrium" title="Bohrium">bohrium</a>), 108 (<a href="/wiki/Hassium" title="Hassium">hassium</a>), 109 (<a href="/wiki/Meitnerium" title="Meitnerium">meitnerium</a>), 110 (<a href="/wiki/Darmstadtium" title="Darmstadtium">darmstadtium</a>), 111 (<a href="/wiki/Roentgenium" title="Roentgenium">roentgenium</a>) and 112 (<a href="/wiki/Copernicium" title="Copernicium">copernicium</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hans_Busch" title="Hans Busch">Hans Busch</a>, pioneer of <a href="/wiki/Electron_optics" title="Electron optics">electron optics</a> and laid the theoretical basis for the <a href="/wiki/Electron_microscope" title="Electron microscope">electron microscope</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paolo_Giubellino" title="Paolo Giubellino">Paolo Giubellino</a>, Scientific Managing Director of the <a href="/wiki/Facility_for_Antiproton_and_Ion_Research" title="Facility for Antiproton and Ion Research">Facility for Antiproton and Ion Research</a> and the <a href="/wiki/GSI_Helmholtz_Centre_for_Heavy_Ion_Research" title="GSI Helmholtz Centre for Heavy Ion Research">GSI Helmholtz Centre for Heavy Ion Research</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_Bibel" title="Wolfgang Bibel">Wolfgang Bibel</a>, one of the founders of the research area of <a href="/wiki/Artificial_Intelligence" class="mw-redirect" title="Artificial Intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> in <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> and <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ottmar_Edenhofer" title="Ottmar Edenhofer">Ottmar Edenhofer</a>, lead author of the reports published by the <a href="/wiki/Intergovernmental_Panel_on_Climate_Change" title="Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change">Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change</a> which was awarded the Nobel Peace Prize (2007)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mohan_Munasinghe" title="Mohan Munasinghe">Mohan Munasinghe</a>, vice-chairman of the Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change which was awarded the Nobel Peace Prize (2007)<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Andreas Dreizler, mechanical engineer and <a href="/wiki/Gottfried_Wilhelm_Leibniz_Prize" title="Gottfried Wilhelm Leibniz Prize">Leibniz Prize</a> laureate (2014)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rainer_Waser" title="Rainer Waser">Rainer Waser</a>, electrical engineer and Leibniz Prize laureate (2014)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lutz_Raphael" title="Lutz Raphael">Lutz Raphael</a>, historian and Leibniz Prize laureate (2013)</li>
<li>Jürgen Eckert, engineer and Leibniz Prize laureate (2009)</li>
<li>Jürgen Rödel, material scientist and Leibniz Prize laureate (2009)</li>
<li>Thomas Weiland, physicist and Leibniz Prize laureate (1998)</li>
<li>Johannes Buchmann, computer scientist, mathematician and Leibniz Prize laureate (1993)</li>
<li>Randolf Menzel, zoologist and Leibniz Prize laureate (1991)</li>
<li>Thomas Weiland, physicist and Leibniz Prize laureate (1988)</li>
<li>Wolfram Saenger, biochemist and Leibniz Prize laureate (1988)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernd_Giese" title="Bernd Giese">Bernd Giese</a>, chemist and Leibniz Prize laureate (1987)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Frank_Steglich" title="Frank Steglich">Frank Steglich</a>, physicist and Leibniz Prize laureate (1986)</li>
<li>Eric Bodden, <a href="/wiki/Heinz_Maier-Leibnitz-Preis" title="Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis">Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis</a> laureate (2014)</li>
<li>Stefan Roth, Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis laureate (2012)</li>
<li>Christina Thiele, Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis laureate (2010)</li>
<li>Torsten Granzow, Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis laureate (2008)</li>
<li>Nicole Deitelhoff, Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis laureate (2008)</li>
<li>Marc Alexa, Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis laureate (2003)</li>
<li>Carsten Bolm, Heinz Maier-Leibnitz-Preis laureate (1991)</li>
<li>Alexandre Obertelli, Alexander von Humboldt Professorship of the <a href="/wiki/Alexander_von_Humboldt_Foundation" title="Alexander von Humboldt Foundation">Alexander-von-Humboldt-Stiftung</a> (2019)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Johann-Dietrich_W%C3%B6rner" title="Johann-Dietrich Wörner">Johann Dietrich Wörner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Director_General_of_the_European_Space_Agency" title="Director General of the European Space Agency">Director General of the European Space Agency</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kurt_H._Debus" title="Kurt H. Debus">Kurt H. Debus</a>, rocket scientist and first <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">Kennedy Space Center</a> director</li>
<li>Robert Piloty, pioneer of computer engineering and one of the founding fathers of computer science courses in Germany</li>
<li>Peter Mertens, one of the founding fathers of <a href="/wiki/Business_informatics" title="Business informatics">business informatics</a> courses in Germany</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marc_Baldus" title="Marc Baldus">Marc Baldus</a>, physicist and professor of structural biology at <a href="/wiki/Utrecht_University" title="Utrecht University">Utrecht University</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hanns-Peter_Boehm" title="Hanns-Peter Boehm">Hanns-Peter Boehm</a>, chemist and a pioneer of <a href="/wiki/Graphene" title="Graphene">graphene</a> research</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sabine_Brunswicker" title="Sabine Brunswicker">Sabine Brunswicker</a>, professor for digital innovation and the Founder and Director of Research Center for Open Digital Innovation (RCODI)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Friedrich_Dessauer" title="Friedrich Dessauer">Friedrich Dessauer</a>, pioneer of X-ray technology</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Dolivo-Dobrovolsky" title="Mikhail Dolivo-Dobrovolsky">Mikhail Dolivo-Dobrovolsky</a>, inventor of the <a href="/wiki/Electrical_motor" class="mw-redirect" title="Electrical motor">three-phase electrical motor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Encarna%C3%A7%C3%A3o" title="José Luis Encarnação">José Luis Encarnação</a>, inventor of the <a href="/wiki/Graphical_Kernel_System" title="Graphical Kernel System">Graphical Kernel System</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paul_Friedl%C3%A4nder_(chemist)" title="Paul Friedländer (chemist)">Paul Friedländer</a>, chemist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kurt_Hohenemser" title="Kurt Hohenemser">Kurt Hohenemser</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aerospace_engineer" class="mw-redirect" title="Aerospace engineer">aerospace engineer</a> and pioneer in helicopter design</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karl_K%C3%BCpfm%C3%BCller" title="Karl Küpfmüller">Karl Küpfmüller</a>, electrical engineer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/El_Lissitzky" title="El Lissitzky">El Lissitzky</a>, architect and designer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ernst_May" title="Ernst May">Ernst May</a>, architect and city planner of <a href="/wiki/New_Frankfurt" title="New Frankfurt">New Frankfurt</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ernst_Neufert" title="Ernst Neufert">Ernst Neufert</a>, architect</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gustav_Niemann" title="Gustav Niemann">Gustav Niemann</a>, mechanical engineer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fritz_von_Opel" title="Fritz von Opel">Fritz von Opel</a> rocket pioneer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Frank_Schimmelfennig" title="Frank Schimmelfennig">Frank Schimmelfennig</a>, political scientist</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernhard_Schlink" title="Bernhard Schlink">Bernhard Schlink</a>, former judge and writer (<a href="/wiki/The_Reader" title="The Reader">The Reader</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ernst_Schr%C3%B6der" title="Ernst Schröder">Ernst Schröder</a>, mathematician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gerhard_M._Sessler" title="Gerhard M. Sessler">Gerhard M. Sessler</a>, inventor of the <a href="/wiki/Electret_microphone" title="Electret microphone">electret microphone</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thomas_Sieverts" title="Thomas Sieverts">Thomas Sieverts</a>, architect and urban planner</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rudolf_Wille" title="Rudolf Wille">Rudolf Wille</a>, mathematician</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hermann_Zapf" title="Hermann Zapf">Hermann Zapf</a>, typeface designer (<a href="/wiki/Palatino" title="Palatino">Palatino</a>, <a href="/wiki/Optima" title="Optima">Optima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zapfino" title="Zapfino">Zapfino</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eduard_Zintl" title="Eduard Zintl">Eduard Zintl</a>, chemist and discoverer of the <a href="/wiki/Zintl_phase" title="Zintl phase">Zintl phase</a></li></ul>
